< review>
I have been using Pico for almost two years now, to provide care for all my rescue dogs...Saving Imperial Rescue.

Dr. Amir and Dr. Arsalan are two of the most compassionate and caring doctors I have ever had the pleasure to work with; they are polite and kind when dealing with animal owners and rescue volunteers. They actually CARE about the animals, and they want to help make vet care affordable for rescues. I cannot say enough about them; if it weren't for them, I truly would never be able to save the animals that I do.

Dr. Amir has also done some dental and orthopedic surgeries that some other vets may not want to attempt, but rather refer to a specialist. What a HUGE cost savings to our rescue.

As a family run business, they do not gouge their customers, and the fact that they have another office in San Clemente (that is open on Sunday), it allows us to have 7 days a week accessibility to medical care when needed.

If I could give Pico Vet and their staff 10 stars, I would!< /review>

<Review>The first thing that came to mind was Jean-Ralphio (Parks n Rec) when I heard "Bel Bacio." But truthfully, I just wanted to find a cafe in downtown San Jose that looked nice and had strong wi-fi (preferably a place I hadn't been to before).

Well, my first impression of Bel Bacio was that it was kinda magical. This was because  Bel Bacio is located in Little Italy (a magical little strip that isn't as interesting as Little Italy in San Diego, but is still special in its own way). Thankfully, there's a good amount of 2-hr (coin) street parking across from Bel Bacio.

Bel Bacio is pretty on the inside, and the employees were both warm and helpful.

I got to try their Nutellino (which is basically an espresso shot with a lot of Nutella and creme). Yup. It was marvelous.

This is a great place to study at not only because it's pretty and quiet but also because the seats are pretty comfy.

< text>
The cookies and the coffee are absolutely fabulous. They taste great. The cookies have that better than home made taste, rich, buttery, delicious. Original flavors too. I recommend the almond and apricot cookies. They have a round chocolate shortbread which is not too sweet, perfect with a creamy latte.

Coffee is served in Italian (plus) sizes, so their largest one is smaller than a small Starbucks. Good flavor, beans definitely not burnt. The setting is nice too, very pleasant and cozy.

4 stars instead of 5 because they should have two people working there. We came in one morning and to get our cookies and coffee it took 26minutes. We know exactly because we put 30m on the parking meter and there were 4m left when we came back. That's too long for coffee, I don't think we would come during the week before work but for the weekend to enjoy la dolce vita, it's perfect.</text>

<Rate>4< /Rate>< review>
Updating my review because I recently ordered an iced mocha and it was almost just like my first one! Only thing they forgot was the whipped cream on top.

Ordered a Fagotto (a chocolate+custard-filled sugary croissant, which is AWESOME). I asked for it warmed up and, unfortunately, they heated it up in the microwave (-1 points). Gotta toaster oven that badboy! Either way, this is a badass dessert. Love the subtle hint of custard in the filling to compliment the rich chocolate syrup.

Ate the fagotto with a side of the PISTACHIO GELATO. Match made in heaven. It was so good! They need to put more fresh salted pistachios in the gelato, though! I only got like 3 nuts total. I wish I had gotten 30 nuts.

I think I let a few poor experiences resulted in my previously bad review. Overall, though, this place is on point!<//review>

< text>
Best stylist for my hair type, ever! I live in Germany and return to get my hair cut annually by Jo Jo because no other stylist compares. I have extremely thick strong Mediterranean-like hair, which only Jo Jo has been able to cut and style to my satisfaction. Ironically, I would've thought I could find someone in Germany who could cut my hair well due to the large presence of Turkish, Greek, and other ethnicities in the population who tend to have my hair type. But after trying different stylists for ten years, I have yet to find a stylist as close to good as Jo Jo. He is able to thin out my thick hair without making me look like a mushroom cap. I always come out of Jo Jo's studio feeling confident and sexy knowing it will grow out nicely, yet hoping it will last until the next time I return to San Jose. I HIGHLY recommend Jo Jo, his products, and his well run salon for anyone who wants to look and feel good by a professional who wants the same for you because it's his passion and he feels good when YOU do. I will keep coming back for as long Jo continues his art!< /text>

<Review>*COVID-19 pandemic review*

It's been about 8 months since my last hair cut with JoJo, so I was so happy he was able to take me for a wash and hair cut on the Saturday during Labor Day weekend (this was right before the county loosened up and allowed 25% indoor services to open). Being five months pregnant, I had been very paranoid and cautious about leaving my house, but I was so relieved to see JoJo take ALL of the precautions to make the experience safe for me and all of his customers. Here's a quick summary of my visit:

- Masks are required to be worn the entire time by the customer and by the stylist

- You fill out a questionnaire about COVID exposure and they take your temperature at the door

- JoJo was frequently sanitizing his hands every few minutes

- His hair cutting station was outdoors on his patio, fully shaded, and he had a fan and air purifier running as well (he told me he after the Labor Day holiday he is allowed to have some stations indoors... which is great because he has 2 rooms in his salon that has big doors that can open up and circulate fresh air)

- His assistant would vacuum cut hair from the floor every few minutes

- Any towels or smocks used for my visit were discarded into a secure covered bin immediately after he was done

- He only took credit card as payment - I wasn't thinking and tried to hand him my CC directly (oops!), but he didn't take it and asked me to insert the card into the chip reader to finish the no-contact payment

I am so happy with my cut. My head feels 10 lbs lighter and for once I was starting to feel some kind of pregnancy 'glow.' I was not able to get my hair colored because of my condition, but what's amazing was the previous colors and highlights he used back in January blended so well with my roots - it's almost as if he designed it so that it could grow out naturally to blend well (minus all the grey hairs)!  I love it.

I am super appreciative of all the steps JoJo and his assistant took to make me feel safe during my visit and am thrilled to be able to support a local business. Even before this pandemic, JoJo had always gone above and beyond to take care of his customers - he's the best at what he does and I will 100% recommend his salon always.<//Review>< username>
Lindrew Lam<//username>

<username>Wyrd Dragon</username><Date>1538153713145< /Date><rate>5< /rate>< text>
Jojo Hair Studio is in all seriousness one of the best salon experiences I've had in 30 years.

I and my spouse came in to fix our hairmergency - our hair desperately needed care, cut, and color.

I'd researched many local salons but the top pick was Jojo Hair Studio. I called and spoke to Ray Ray, who was effervescent, friendly and accommodating, so I went right ahead and booked.

We've now completed the first half of this process (consultation, cut and style) and are looking forward to returning to complete our color plans as well.

The salon itself is an absolutely lovely space -we'd had a stressful day and felt immediately more relaxed and happy upon walking in and being greeted by the staff.

The decor, the layout, and the whole vibe just makes me feel the place is loved and cared for by the owner and staff. It has that special energy, more like an artists studio than 'just' a place of business (and the coffee and biscotti are excellent)

Ray Ray and Rosa gave us both inspired, attentive, and lovely service, and understood exactly what we both wanted to do with our hair. My spouse's long romantic princess hair and my dragon warrior do have never *ever* looked better

We're GNC trans folx who feel best when our outward presentation matches our identity - Ray Ray and Rosa gave us the cut and style of our lives, and made us both look and feel more like our real selves. I've never seen my spouse so happy with their hair, and so pretty!

I myself couldn't be happier with Ray Ray's work on my hair, and his plans for my color - he has a real genius for this work, and I feel so lucky to be able to collaborate with an artist who really *gets* what I'm trying to achieve

I'd recommend Jojo Hair Studio to other LGBTQIA+ people looking for boutique salon treatment in amazing surrounds with inspired artists who care about their work

I'll be returning with another review and before/after pictures when our color is completed :)< /text>

<rating>4</rating>< review>
I got the $6 basic wash. Not bad, my only complaints are that the soap wasn't 100% washed off and the dryers didn't dry completely, left some water spots and the sap and small dirt scratches didn't quite get washed off my car. In my experience these express car washes never 100% wash and dry my car anyways though.

Free vacuums is included even with basic package. They have okay suction but it's a little difficult because they don't have any precision vacuum hoses for the tight cracks. The pressure air hose was necessary to finish drying off my side view mirrors, although they have a package with spot free rinse but I don't know if it works well.

You pay through a kiosk with card (or cash as well I believe) and workers get up to assist you for aligning your car with the belt, and sprayed some water or something around my car to prep it.

Overall, it's pretty much what I expected in an express car wash and I got what I paid for.<//review>
